ATC 240 -District Admin verify whether data is sorted when Clicking on column headers
    [Documentation]    ATC 240 -District Admin verify whether data is sorted when Clicking on column headers
    ...
    ...    Step1 : Login with valid District Admin credentials.
    ...
    ...    Step2 : Navigate to Management.
    ...
    ...    Step3 : verify whether data is sorted when Clicking on column headers for Classes table and All Users table.
    Run Keyword If    '${preDistrictAdminStatus}'=='False'    Fail    PreRequisite District Admin is not created
    ${DistrictAdminUid}    Get From Dictionary    ${preDistrictAdminDetails}    UserName
    ${DistrictAdminPwd}    Get From Dictionary    ${preDistrictAdminDetails}    Password
    Comment    Login into Application with District admin Credentials.
    ${bStatus}=    LoginToWizardApp    ${DistrictAdminUid}    ${DistrictAdminPwd}
    Run Keyword If    '${bStatus}'=='False'    Fail    The user is not able to login with these ctredentials-'${Teacher_userId}','${Teacher_Password}'.
    Comment    Navigate to Management page.
    Navigate To Management Page
    Wait And Select Frame    ${header.management.schoolAdminFrame}
    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${table.classesAndGroups}    ${TimeOut}
    Comment    Sort the Columns of Classes or Groups Table.
    ${classorGroupColumns}=    Create List    Name    Teacher    Description    Class Code    Created
    : FOR    ${cName}    IN    @{classorGroupColumns}
    \    ${columnValues}=    Get Table Values Into List    ${table.classesAndGroups}    ${cName}
    \    Sort List    ${columnValues}
    \    Log    ${columnValues}
    \    Table Column Values Sorting    ${table.classesAndGroups}    ${cName}    ascend
    \    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${table.classesAndGroups}//th[contains(@class,'sort-up') and contains(text(),'${cName}')]    ${TimeOut}
    \    ${ascendColumnValues}=    Get Table Values Into List    ${table.classesAndGroups}    ${cName}
    \    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Lists Should Be Equal    ${columnValues}    ${ascendColumnValues}
    \    Reverse List    ${columnValues}
    \    Table Column Values Sorting    ${table.classesAndGroups}    ${cName}
    \    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${table.classesAndGroups}//th[contains(@class,'sort-down') and contains(text(),'${cName}')]    ${TimeOut}
    \    ${descendColumnValues}=    Get Table Values Into List    ${table.classesAndGroups}    ${cName}
    \    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Lists Should Be Equal    ${columnValues}    ${descendColumnValues}
    Comment    Sort the Columns of 'All Users' Table.
    ${usersTableColumns}=    Create List    Last Name    First Name    Grade    Status    Role
    ...    Created
    : FOR    ${cName}    IN    @{usersTableColumns}
    \    ${columnValues}=    Get Table Values Into List    ${table.users}    ${cName}
    \    Sort List    ${columnValues}
    \    Log    ${columnValues}
    \    Table Column Values Sorting    ${table.users}    ${cName}    ascend
    \    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${table.users}//th[contains(@class,'sort-up') and contains(text(),'${cName}')]    ${TimeOut}
    \    ${ascendColumnValues}=    Get Table Values Into List    ${table.users}    ${cName}
    \    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Lists Should Be Equal    ${columnValues}    ${ascendColumnValues}
    \    Reverse List    ${columnValues}
    \    Table Column Values Sorting    ${table.users}    ${cName}
    \    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${table.users}//th[contains(@class,'sort-down') and contains(text(),'${cName}')]    ${TimeOut}
    \    ${descendColumnValues}=    Get Table Values Into List    ${table.users}    ${cName}
    \    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Lists Should Be Equal    ${columnValues}    ${descendColumnValues}
    [Teardown]    Stop Application

ATC 231 District Admin-Reports generation verification with lateral from date compared to the to date
    [Documentation]    ATC 231 District admin - Reports generation with from date lateral one than to date
    ...
    ...    Step1 : Login to wizard application as an district admin and navigate to "Reports Filter" page.
    ...
    ...    Step2 : Select all the report filters for "standard Mastery" report.
    ...
    ...    Step3 : Enter the past date in the "to date" \ then "This value is out of range" tooltip should be displayed.
    ...
    ...    Step4 : Click on "Generate Report" button then it should navigate you to the reports page.
    ...
    ...    Step5 : It should display an error message.
    ${AssignmentNameTitle}    Set Variable    @{preSignUpTitleMenus}[1]
    ${className}    Set Variable    @{preClassesList}[1]
    ${DistrictAdminUid}    Get From Dictionary    ${preDistrictAdminDetails}    UserName
    ${DistrictAdminPwd}    Get From Dictionary    ${preDistrictAdminDetails}    Password
    Comment    Login into Application with District admin Credentials.
    ${loginStatus}    LoginToWizardApp    ${DistrictAdminUid}    ${DistrictAdminPwd}
    Run Keyword Unless    ${loginStatus}    Fail    School admin is unable to login with valid credentials.
    ${reportType}    Set Variable    ${preReportType1}
    ${toDate}    Get Current Date
    ${Dates}=    Split String    ${toDate}    /
    ${Date}=    Evaluate    ${Dates[0]}+1
    ${fromDate}=    Set Variable    ${Date}/${Dates[1]}/${Dates[2]}
    Comment    To navigate to report filters page
    Navigate To Report Filters Page
    Comment    Select Standards Mastery Report,School,class and subject from the drop down.
    Select The Drop Down Value    Report Type    ${reportType}
    Select The Drop Down Value    School    ${preSchoolName}
    Select The Drop Down Value    Classes    ${className}
    Select The Drop Down Value    Subject/Level    ${AssignmentNameTitle}
    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${textbox.reports.myFromDate}    ${TimeOut}
    Comment    Enter from date and To date into the text fields
    Input Text    ${textbox.reports.myFromDate}    ${fromDate}
    Input Text    ${textbox.reports.myToDate}    ${toDate}
    ${toolTipStatus}    Verify Element Visible    ${label.signUp.toolTipText}
    Comment    Verify whether the "Date out of range" tooltip is displayed or not.
    ${genBtnStatus}    Verify Element Visible    ${button.reports.Generate Report}
    Run Keyword If    '${toolTipStatus}'!='True' and '${genBtnStatus}'!='True'    Fail    Tool tip and Generate button both are not displayed when enter From date is greater than Todate.
    ${toolTipMsg}    Run Keyword If    ${toolTipStatus}    Get Text    ${label.signUp.toolTipText}
    Run Keyword If    "${toolTipMsg}"=="None"    Fail    The "date out of range" alert is not displayed.
    Sleep    3s
    Run Keyword Unless    ${genBtnStatus}    Fail    The"Generate Report" button is not visible when we enter from date later one compared to the to date
    Navigate To Reports Page
    Comment    Verify whether it navigates to "Reports" page or not when we enter invalid date range
    ${bStatus}    Run Keyword And Return Status    Wait And Select Frame    iframeReport    ${TimeOut}
    Run Keyword If    ${bStatus}    Fail    The "Generate Report" button navigates the page to "Reports" page when we enter from date later one compared to the to date
    [Teardown]    Stop Application

    ...    Steps:
    ...    1. Login to the wizard application as a teacher.
    ...    2. Click on "help" menu and verify "quicktips" page.
    ...    3. Navigate to the management page.
    ...    4. Click on "help" menu and verify "quicktips" page.
    ...    5. Validate whether quick tips page is refreshing or not when switching to different pages.
    Run Keyword If    '${preTeacherID}'=='${EMPTY}'    Fail    PreRequisite teacher is not created
    ${teacherUID}    Set Variable    ${preTeacherID}
    ${teacherPwd}    Set Variable    ${preTeacherPassword}
    Comment    Login with Valid Teacher Credentials.
    ${loginStatus}    LoginToWizardApp    ${teacherUID}    ${teacherPwd}
    Run Keyword If    ${loginStatus}==False    Fail    The user is not able to login with valid credentials.
    Comment    Select help menu and click on sub menu "quickTips".
    Wait And Click Element    ${button.home.help}    ${TimeOut}    Help
    ${bStatus}    Verify Element Visible    ${link.home.quickTips}
    Run Keyword If    ${bStatus}    Wait And Click Element    ${link.home.quickTips}
    ${emailSupportWind}    Verify Element Visible    ${header.home.help.quickTipsWindowClose}
    Run Keyword Unless    ${emailSupportWind}    Fail    The "Quick tips" window is not displayed.
    Wait And Select Frame    ${label.quickTipsFrame.quickTips}
    ${status}    Verify Element Visible    //b[contains(text(),'Teacher View')]
    ${bStatus}    Verify Element Visible    //p/font[@size="5"]/b[contains(text(),'Management')]
    Wait Until Element Is Visible    //span[contains(text(),'Quick Tips')]/following-sibling::span    ${TimeOut}
    Wait Until Keyword Succeeds    2m    2s    Wait And Click Element    //span[contains(text(),'Quick Tips')]/following-sibling::span
    Unselect Frame
    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Run Keyword If    ${status} and ${bStatus}    Fail    Teacher View and Management views are displayed.
    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Run Keyword If    '${status}'!='True' and '${bStatus}'='True'    Fail    Teacher View and Management views are not displayed.
    Comment    Navigate to the management page.
    Navigate To Management Page
    Comment    Select help menu and click on sub menu "quickTips".
    Wait And Click Element    ${button.management.help}    ${TimeOut}    Help
    ${bStatus}    Verify Element Visible    ${link.home.quickTips}
    Run Keyword If    ${bStatus}    Click Element    ${link.home.quickTips}
    ${emailSupportWind}    Verify Element Visible    ${header.home.help.quickTipsWindowClose}
    Run Keyword Unless    ${emailSupportWind}    Fail    The "Quick tips" window is not displayed in management page.
    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${header.home.help.quickTipsWindowClose}    ${TimeOut}
    Wait And Select Frame    ${label.quickTipsFrame.quickTips}
    ${status}    Verify Element Visible    //b[contains(text(),'Teacher View')]
    ${bStatus}    Verify Element Visible    //p/font[@size="5"]/b[contains(text(),'Management')]
    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Run Keyword If    ${status} and ${bStatus}    Fail    Teacher View and Management views are displayed.
    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Run Keyword If    '${status}'!='True' and '${bStatus}'='True'    Fail    Teacher View and Management views are not displayed.
    [Teardown]    Stop Application

ATC 428 - Verify whether Same registration code is accepting for multiple times or not.
    [Documentation]    ATC 428 - Verify whether Same registration code is accepting for multiple times or not.
    ...    Steps:
    ...    1. Login to the wizard application as a teacher.
    ...    2. Navigate to the management page.
    ...    3. Select the teacher role from user details.
    ...    4. Click on "Edit" button and then click on "Add" button.
    ...    5. Enter the registration code and select the title.
    ...    6. Click on "Next" button.
    ...    7. Click on "add" button.
    ...    8. Enter the same registration code and verify whether same registration code is accepting for multiple times or not.
    Run Keyword If    '${preTeacherID}'=='${EMPTY}'    Fail    PreRequisite teacher is not created
    Comment    Login with Valid Teacher Credentials.

    Navigate To Management Page

    Wait And Select Frame    ${header.management.schoolAdminFrame}
    Select The Record In Table    ${table.users}    Role    Teacher
    Comment    Enter the registration code into registration Field and Select Assessment Title from dropdown.
    Wait And Click Element    ${button.userDetails.edit}
    Wait And Click Element    ${button.Details.AddRegCode}
    ${teacherRegCode}    Get Teacher Registration Code    ${CODES_URL}
    Run Keyword If    '${BROWSER}'=='ie'    TypeCharactertoTextBox    ${text.management.addTeCode}    ${teacherRegCode}
    Run Keyword If    '${BROWSER}'!='ie'    Enter Text In Text Field    ${text.management.addTeCode}    ${teacherRegCode}
    ${AssignmentTitle}    Set Variable    CCS Motivation Math Level 05
    Wait And Click Element    ${table.management.chooseTitleArrowButton}
    ${SignUpTitleMenuStatus}    Run Keyword And Return Status    Wait Until Element Is Visible    //td[contains(@id,'dijit_MenuItem') and contains(text(),'${AssignmentTitle}')]
    Run Keyword If    ${SignUpTitleMenuStatus}    Wait And Click Element    //td[contains(@id,'dijit_MenuItem') and contains(text(),'${AssignmentTitle}')]
    ${bStatus}=    Run Keyword And Return Status    Wait Until Element Is Visible    //div/span[contains(text(),'Choose a title')]
    Run Keyword If    ${SignUpTitleMenuStatus}==True and ${bStatus}!=True    Wait And Click Element    ${button.signUp.next}
    Comment    Enter the registration code into registration Field and Select Assessment Title from dropdown.
    ${AssignmentTitle}    Set Variable    CCS Reading Assessments Level 5
    Wait And Click Element    ${button.Details.AddRegCode}
    Run Keyword If    '${BROWSER}'=='ie'    TypeCharactertoTextBox    ${text.management.addTeCode}    ${teacherRegCode}
    Run Keyword If    '${BROWSER}'!='ie'    Enter Text In Text Field    ${text.management.addTeCode}    ${teacherRegCode}
    Comment    Verify whether Same registration code is accepting for multiple times or not.
    Run Keyword And Continue On Failure    Wait Until Element Is Visible    ${label.signUp.toolTipText}    5s
    Sleep    10s
    ${toolTipMsg2}    Get Text    ${label.signUp.toolTipText}
    ${errorMsg}    Run Keyword And Return Status    Should Contain    ${toolTipMsg2}    Registration Code not recognized
    Run Keyword Unless    ${errorMsg}    Fail    Same registration codes are accepting.
    [Teardown]    Stop Application
